# CleanSlate: These on_bi_yearly_pulse and on_five_year_pulse events frequently check for character modifiers they add that last for under year...

### Lustful positive ###
character_event = {
	id = 3000
	desc = EVTDESC3000
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		in_command_trigger = no
		trait = lustful
		NOT = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }

		job_spiritual = {
			is_adult = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gluttonous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = greedy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = temperate
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = charitable
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3000

		piety = 10
		remove_trait = lustful

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_approves
			who = job_spiritual
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3000

		piety = -5

		random = {
			chance = 15
			add_trait_fully_deceitful_effect = yes
		}

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_lying_about_confession
			who = job_spiritual
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

### Lustful negative ###
character_event = {
	id = 3001
	desc = EVTDESC3001
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = lustful
		in_command_trigger = no

		OR = {
			any_courtier = {
				trait = lustful
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 50
				}
			}

			spouse = {
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = greedy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = envious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = charitable
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = kind
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3001

		scaled_wealth = -0.10
	}
}

### Lustful positive ###
character_event = {
	id = 3005
	desc = EVTDESC3005
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = lustful
		in_command_trigger = no

		NOR = {
			trait = wounded
			trait = craven
		}

		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_married = no }

			any_courtier = {
				is_female = yes
				practical_age < 35
				block_general_event_trigger = no

				NOR = {
					is_close_relative = ROOT
					trait = ugly
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = patient
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				practical_age < 35
				block_general_event_trigger = no

				NOR = {
					is_close_relative = ROOT
					trait = ugly
				}
			}

			preferred_limit = {
				is_attractive_trigger = yes
			}

			save_event_target_as = scoped_lady
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3005

		trigger = { is_married = no }

		prestige = 15

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_tourney_boost
			who = event_target:scoped_lady
			years = 5
		}

		# random = {
		# 	chance = 10
		# 	add_trait_wounded_effect = yes
		# }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3005

		trigger = { is_married = yes }

		prestige = 15

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_tourney_boost
			who = spouse
			years = 5
		}

		random = {
			chance = 10
			add_trait_wounded_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3005

		prestige = -5

		random = {
			chance = 10
			add_trait_fully_craven_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

### Lustful negative ###
character_event = {
	id = 3010
	desc = EVTDESC3010
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = lustful
		in_command_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }
		job_spiritual = { character = yes }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = slothful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = envious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = kind
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3010

		piety = -15

		job_spiritual = {
			show_scope_change = no

			prestige = 15
		}
	}
}

### CHASTE ###

### Chaste positive ###
character_event = {
	id = 3020
	desc = EVTDESC3020
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		in_command_trigger = no
		controls_religion = no

		NOR = {
			trait = excommunicated
			religion = messalian
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = slothful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = humble
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_children = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3020

		trigger = {
			lifestyle_traits < 1
			is_married = yes
		}

		piety = 20
		add_trait_silently_celibate_effect = yes

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3020
		tooltip_info = cynical

		trigger = { trait = cynical }

		remove_trait = chaste
		piety = -5
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3020

		any_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no

				OR = {
					trait = lustful
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_despise_chaste
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}

		piety = 10
		prestige = 5
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3020

		piety = 5
	}
}

### Chaste Positive (create character) ###
character_event = {
	id = 3021
	desc = EVTDESC3021
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		piety >= 25
		in_command_trigger = no

		NOR = {
			trait = excommunicated
			trait = cynical
			religion = messalian
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = slothful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = crusader
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = zealous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = just
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3021

		create_character = {
			female = no
			dynasty = random
			age = 55
			culture = ROOT
			religion = ROOT

			attributes = {
				learning = 9
			}

			add_trait = chaste
			add_trait = zealous
			add_trait = celibate
			add_trait = mastermind_theologian
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3021

		piety = 5
	}
}

### Old scholar ###
character_event = {
	id = 3022
	desc = EVTDESC3022
	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 25
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		NOT = { trait = excommunicated }

		any_courtier = {
			trait = celibate
			is_female = no
			learning >= 9
			practical_age >= 55
			trait = chaste
			trait = zealous
			prisoner = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = zealous
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3022

		change_learning = 1

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = chaste_learning
			years = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3022

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				trait = celibate
				is_female = no
				learning >= 9
				practical_age >= 55
				trait = chaste
				trait = zealous
				prisoner = no
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_chaste_advice_refused
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
		}

		remove_trait = chaste
	}
}

### Chaste positive ###
character_event = {
	id = 3025
	desc = EVTDESC3025
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		in_command_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = yes
			age >= 18
			practical_age < 35
			fertility >= 0.40
			is_married = no
			is_pregnant = no
			prisoner = no

			NOR = {
				trait = celibate
				trait = homosexual
				is_close_relative = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = patient
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				age >= 18
				practical_age < 35
				fertility >= 0.40
				is_married = no
				is_pregnant = no
				prisoner = no

				NOR = {
					trait = celibate
					trait = homosexual
					is_close_relative = ROOT
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = scoped_lady
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3025

		prestige = 5
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3025

		piety = 5
	}

	after = {
		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_admire_chaste
			who = event_target:scoped_lady
			years = 15
		}
	}
}

### Cornered by woman ###
character_event = {
	id = 3026
	desc = EVTDESC3026
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		fertility >= 0.40
		in_command_trigger = no

		NOR = {
			trait = celibate
			trait = homosexual
			trait = eunuch
		}

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = yes
			age >= 18
			practical_age < 35
			is_married = no
			is_pregnant = no
			fertility >= 0.40
			prisoner = no

			has_opinion_modifier = {
				name = opinion_admire_chaste
				who = ROOT
			}

			NOR = {
				trait = celibate
				trait = homosexual
				is_close_relative = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				age >= 18
				practical_age < 35
				is_married = no
				is_pregnant = no
				fertility >= 0.40
				prisoner = no

				has_opinion_modifier = {
					name = opinion_admire_chaste
					who = ROOT
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = celibate
					trait = homosexual
					is_close_relative = ROOT
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = lovely_lady
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = patient
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTA3026
			trigger = { religion_group = christian }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTC3026
			trigger = {
				NOT = { religion_group = christian }
			}
		}

		event_target:lovely_lady = {
			show_scope_change = no

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_married = yes
						is_consort = yes
					}
				}
				impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				impregnate = ROOT
			}
		}

		add_trait_silently_stressed_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3026

		reverse_remove_opinion = {
			name = opinion_admire_chaste
			who = event_target:lovely_lady
		}

		prestige = -5
		add_trait_fully_silently_wroth_effect = yes
	}
}

### Chaste negative ###
character_event = {
	id = 3030
	desc = EVTDESC3030
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	rivals = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		has_nickname = no
		prestige < 200
		in_command_trigger = no
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = deceitful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = honest
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3030

		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }

			random_rival = {
				show_scope_change = no

				prestige = 10
			}

			give_nickname = nick_the_effeminate
			piety = -10
		}
		else = {
			random_rival = {
				show_scope_change = no

				prestige = 10
			}

			random = {
				chance = 25

				give_nickname = nick_the_effeminate
				prestige = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

### Chaste negative ###
character_event = {
	id = 3035
	desc = EVTDESC3035
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = chaste
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_married = no }

			any_courtier = {
				is_female = yes
				is_adult = yes
				practical_age < 35
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = gluttonous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = poet
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = scholar
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = mystic
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				is_adult = yes
				practical_age < 35
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			}

			save_event_target_as = scoped_lady
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3035

		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_married = no }
				religion_group = christian
			}
			trigger_else = {
				religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 25
			add_trait_fully_lustful_effect = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = christian }
			piety = -25
		}
		else = {
			piety = 25
		}

		event_target:scoped_lady = {
			show_scope_change = no

			hidden_effect = {
				random = {
					chance = 20
					impregnate_cuckoo = ROOT
				}
			}

			add_trait_fully_silently_lustful_effect = yes

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_infatuated
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3035

		trigger = { is_married = yes }

		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
			piety = 10
		}

		prestige = -25

		random = {
			chance = 5
			remove_trait_chaste_effect = yes
		}

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

character_event = {
	id = 3012
	desc = EVTDESC3012
	picture = GFX_evt_melee
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_economy

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = temperate
		in_command_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no
			martial >= 8
			is_adult = yes
			religion_group = christian
			prisoner = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				martial >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				religion_group = christian
				prisoner = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = target_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3012

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = temperate_good_judgement
			who = event_target:target_courtier
			years = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = { trait = just }
			prestige = 5
		}

		wealth = -20

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5

			trigger = {
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				wealth < 25
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3012

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = defer_to_church_decision
			years = 1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1

			trigger = {
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3012

		wealth = 50
		remove_trait = temperate
		add_trait_fully_silently_greedy_effect = yes
		remove_trait_silently_just_effect = yes

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = temperate_bad_judgement
			who = event_target:target_courtier
			years = 2
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3070
	desc = EVTDESC3070
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_economy

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = greedy
		NOT = { trait = craven }
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			age >= 20
			practical_age < 70

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_female = yes }

				OR = {
					has_religion_feature = religion_matriarchal
					has_religion_feature = religion_equal
					has_religion_feature = religion_feature_bon
					has_law = status_of_women_4
					has_gender_equal_game_rule_trigger = yes
				}
			}

			prisoner = no
			is_incapable = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = patient
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				practical_age >= 20
				practical_age < 70

				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }

					OR = {
						has_religion_feature = religion_matriarchal
						has_religion_feature = religion_equal
						has_religion_feature = religion_feature_bon
						has_law = status_of_women_4
						has_gender_equal_game_rule_trigger = yes
					}
				}

				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no
			}

			preferred_limit = {
				trait = hunter
			}

			preferred_limit = {
				trait = brave
			}

			preferred_limit = {
				NOT = { trait = craven }
			}

			save_event_target_as = hunting_partner
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3070

		show_portrait = event_target:hunting_partner

		event_target:hunting_partner = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3071
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3071
			}
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 99 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3070

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}

			add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = slothful }
			}

			add_trait_fully_silently_slothful_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			prestige = -15
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

### Caring for sick and infirm ###
character_event = {
	id = 3081
	desc = EVTDESC3081
	picture = GFX_evt_illness
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		trait = charitable
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				is_ill = yes
				health_traits >= 1
			}

			is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

			NOT = {
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					name = charitable_to_you
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_ill = yes
					health_traits >= 1
				}

				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						name = charitable_to_you
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = ill_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3081

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = charitable_to_you
			who = event_target:ill_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3081

		trigger = {
			personality_traits < 6
			NOT = { trait = proud }
		}

		opinion = {
			who = ROOT
			name = charitable_to_you
		}

		add_trait_silently_humble_effect = yes
		piety = 10

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = charitable_to_you
			who = event_target:ill_courtier
		}
	}
}

				name = diligent_liege_size

### Envy someone's martial abilities... ###
character_event = {
	id = 3140
	desc = EVTDESC3140
	picture = GFX_evt_melee

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = envious
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no
			martial >= ROOT
			is_adult = yes
			is_ruler = no
			is_incapable = no
			prisoner = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				martial >= ROOT
				is_adult = yes
				is_ruler = no
				is_incapable = no
				prisoner = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = target_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3140

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = envious_neg
			who = event_target:target_courtier
			years = 10
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				personality_traits < 6

				NOR = {
					trait = proud
					trait = wroth
				}
			}

			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				30 = { add_trait_fully_proud_effect = yes }
				20 = { add_trait_fully_wroth_effect = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3140

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = envious_pos
			who = event_target:target_courtier
			years = 10
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				personality_traits < 6

				NOR = {
					trait = deceitful
					trait = humble
				}
			}

			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				30 = { add_trait_fully_deceitful_effect = yes }
				20 = { add_trait_fully_humble_effect = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3140

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = ambitious
				trait = proud
				trait = brave
				trait = zealous
			}
		}

		change_martial = 1

		random = {
			chance = 15
			add_trait_stressed_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

### I have no children, and other women do... ###
character_event = {
	id = 3145
	desc = EVTDESC3145
	picture = GFX_evt_child_play

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_women = yes
	is_married = no
	max_age = 44
	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = envious
		has_children = no
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = yes
			has_children = yes
			is_adult = yes

			age_diff = {
				who = ROOT
				years >= 5
			}

			NOT = { is_older_than = ROOT }
			is_ruler = no
			prisoner = no
			is_incapable = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				has_children = yes
				is_adult = yes
				is_ruler = no

				age_diff = {
					who = ROOT
					years >= 5
				}

				NOT = { is_older_than = ROOT }
				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = young_mother
		}
	}

	option = {

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes

	war = no

		in_command_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			prisoner = no
			is_incapable = no

			NOR = {
				trait = envious
				has_character_modifier = modifier_positive
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = kind
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = charitable
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = envious
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3160

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {

				prisoner = no
				is_incapable = no

				}
			}

			}
		}
	}

		}

character_event = {

			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = kind }
			prisoner = no
			is_incapable = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0

		}

		}

			factor = 0.2

# CleanSlate: Merged with event 3730
character_event = {
	id = 3190

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC3190
		picture = GFX_evt_bishop
		trigger = { religion_group = christian }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC3730
		picture = GFX_evt_scandal
		trigger = { religion_group = muslim }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = wroth
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			religion_group = muslim
		}

		any_courtier = {
			is_abroad = no
			religion_group = ROOT
			block_general_event_trigger = no

			OR = {
				trait = kind
				trait = charitable
				prestige >= 60
			}

			NOR = {
				trait = wroth
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			is_priest = no
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			is_weak_trigger = yes
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = scholarly_theologian
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = mastermind_theologian
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTA3190
			trigger = { religion_group = christian }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTA3730
			trigger = { religion_group = muslim }
		}

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_abroad = no
				religion_group = ROOT
				block_general_event_trigger = no

				OR = {
					trait = kind
					trait = charitable
					prestige >= 60
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = wroth
					trait = patient
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { religion_group = christian }
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIP3191 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIP3731 }
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3191
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 10
			has_ambition = obj_buddhist_reject_pride
		}
	}

	prisoner = no

		}

				name = show_true_humility

			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

		name = EVTOPTA3240 # Submit

		piety = 5

			opinion = {
				name = show_true_humility
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}

			letter_event = {
				id = 3241
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3241
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3240 # NOT submit

		prestige = 5
	}
}

### Limit my ambition ###
character_event = {
	id = 3258
	desc = EVTDESC3258
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		trait = humble
		trait = ambitious

		NAND = {
			martial >= 7
			learning >= 7
			intrigue >= 7
			diplomacy >= 7
			stewardship >= 7
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3258

		remove_trait = ambitious
		piety = 5

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3258

		remove_trait = humble
		piety = -5
	}
}

### Hide martial ###
character_event = {
	id = 3260
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC3260 # Hide martial
		trigger = { religion_group = christian }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC3264
		trigger = {
			NOT = { religion_group = christian }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = deceitful
		martial < 7

		job_marshal = {
			martial >= 10
			martial >= ROOT
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = deceitful_martial }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3260 # Appear to be X

		any_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				OR = {
					martial >= 10
					trait = honest
				}

				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { has_job_title = job_marshal }
			}

			opinion = {
				name = deceitful_neg
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = deceitful_martial
			years = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3260 # Setup job for the blame

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = deceitful_neg
			who = job_marshal
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

### Offend another courtier of a trait we dont have ###
character_event = {
	id = 3280
	desc = EVTDESC3280
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = honest
		NOT = { trait = shy }
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = honest }
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { trait = gluttonous }
				ROOT = { NOT = { trait = gluttonous } }
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = slothful }
				ROOT = { NOT = { trait = slothful } }
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = greedy }
				ROOT = { NOT = { trait = greedy } }
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { trait = envious }
				ROOT = { NOT = { trait = envious } }
			}
			trigger_else = {
				trait = lustful
				ROOT = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = cruel
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3280

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				block_general_event_trigger = no
				NOT = { trait = honest }

				trigger_if = {
					limit = { trait = gluttonous }
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = gluttonous } }
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { trait = slothful }
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = slothful } }
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { trait = greedy }
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = greedy } }
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { trait = envious }
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = envious } }
				}
				trigger_else = {
					trait = lustful
					ROOT = { NOT = { trait = lustful } }
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3281
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3281
			}

			opinion = {
				name = honest_neg
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3280

		random = {
			chance = 15
			add_trait_stressed_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

		name = EVTOPTB3282

	}
}

			}

		}

			factor = 5.0

		}

	}
}

		text = EVTDESC3735
		trigger = { religion_group = muslim }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = craven
		real_tier = COUNT
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		OR = {
			religion_group = christian
			religion_group = muslim
		}

		any_courtier = {
			is_priest = yes
			religion_group = christian
			block_general_event_trigger = no
			NOT = { trait = brave }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = gluttonous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = kind
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTA3305
			trigger = { religion_group = christian }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTA3735
			trigger = { religion_group = muslim }
		}

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_priest = yes
				religion_group = christian
				block_general_event_trigger = no
				NOT = { trait = brave }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { religion_group = christian }
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIP3306 }
			}

				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIP3736 }
			}

				id = 3306
				days = 1
				random = 2
			}
		}
	}

character_event = {
	id = 3320
	desc = EVTDESC3320
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = brave
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no
			age >= 20
			is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

			NAND = {
				trait = brave
				martial >= 7
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = greedy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = humble
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = chaste
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age = 20
				is_female = no
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

				NAND = {
					trait = brave
					martial >= 7
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = nagging_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3320

		event_target:nagging_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3321
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3321
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3320

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = event_target:nagging_courtier
			years = 1
		}
	}
}

	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

			higher_real_tier_than = COUNT
			prestige >= 500
		}

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				trait = ambitious
				trait = diligent
				trait = envious
			}

			is_adult = yes
			prisoner = no
			is_incapable = no
		}
	}

		factor = 1

			factor = 0.3
			trait = patient
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			trait = humble
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = greedy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = wroth
		}

	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = arbitrary
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				trait = envious
				trait = just
				trait = gregarious
			}

			in_command_trigger = no
			block_general_event_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = greedy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = patient
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3405

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = envious
					trait = just
					trait = gregarious
				}

				in_command_trigger = no
				block_general_event_trigger = no
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3406
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3406
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3435
	desc = EVTDESC3435
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_five_year_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		trait = just
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 30
			}

			in_command_trigger = no
			block_general_event_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = envious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 30
				}

				in_command_trigger = no
				block_general_event_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = farmer_dispute_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3435

		event_target:farmer_dispute_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = farmer_wrong

			character_event = {
				id = 3436
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3436
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3435

		event_target:farmer_dispute_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = farmer_correct

			character_event = {
				id = 3436
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3436
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3440
	desc = EVTDESC3440
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_five_year_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		trait = cynical
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = the_cynical }

		any_courtier = {
			wealth >= 20
			in_command_trigger = no
			block_general_event_trigger = no
			NOT = { trait = cynical }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			trait = greedy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = kind
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = patient
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3440

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				wealth >= 20
				in_command_trigger = no
				block_general_event_trigger = no
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3441
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3441
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3470
	desc = EVTDESC3470
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_five_year_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = zealous
		in_command_trigger = no

		OR = {
			spouse = {
				is_abroad = no
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}

			any_child = {
				practical_age >= 15
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = gluttonous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = envious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = kind
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				practical_age >= 15
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
				religion_group = christian

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = nonzealous_child
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3470

		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
				religion_group = christian

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}
		}

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3471
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3471
				portrait = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3470

		trigger = {
			event_target:nonzealous_child = { always = yes }
		}

		event_target:nonzealous_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3471
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB3471
				portrait = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 4.0
			trait = charitable
		}

			factor = 4.0
			trait = patient
		}

		}

# Celibate
character_event = {
	id = 3520
	desc = EVTDESC3520
	picture = GFX_evt_quarrel
	portrait = spouse

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	is_married = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = celibate
		has_lover = no
		in_command_trigger = no
		NOT = { trait = eunuch }

		OR = {
			piety >= 50
			trait = chaste
			trait = humble
		}

		spouse = {
			has_lover = no
			is_pregnant = no
			is_abroad = no
			prisoner = no

			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						trait = chaste
						trait = celibate
					}
				}

				OR = {
					trait = lustful
					trait = hedonist
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			diplomacy >= 8
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		spouse = {
			save_event_target_as = sex_partner
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3520

		piety = 10

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3521
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3521
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_spurned
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3520

		remove_trait = celibate
		piety = -10
		add_lover = spouse
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3520

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = spouse
					value >= 30
				}

				opinion = {
					who = spouse
					value >= 30
				}
			}
		}

		remove_trait = celibate
		piety = -10
		add_lover = spouse
		hidden_effect = { unprotected_sex_effect_event_target = yes }
	}
}

# Celibate: Spouse
character_event = {
	id = 3521
	desc = EVTDESC3521
	picture = GFX_evt_quarrel

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3521

		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = christian }
			add_trait_fully_silently_chaste_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { religion_group = muslim }
			piety = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3521

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_spurned
			who = FROM
			years = 1
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3525
	desc = EVTDESC3525
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	min_age = 27
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = celibate
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { piety < 30 }
			NOT = { trait = lustful }
		}

		any_vassal = {
			trait = chaste
			is_adult = yes
			age < 25

			NOR = {
				trait = celibate
				trait = hedonist
			}

			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
				is_adult = yes
				age < 25

				NOR = {
					trait = celibate
					trait = hedonist
				}

				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = chaste_vassal
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3525

		event_target:chaste_vassal = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3526
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3526
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3525

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = event_target:chaste_vassal
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3525
		tooltip_info = zealous

		trigger = { trait = zealous }

		add_trait_fully_silently_paranoid_effect = yes

		event_target:chaste_vassal = {
			show_scope_change = no

			add_trait_fully_paranoid_effect = yes

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_horrified
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

### Scholar: Gain learning ###
character_event = {
	id = 3540
	desc = EVTDESC3540
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = scholar
		learning < 15
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		NOR = {
			trait = slothful
			trait = content
		}

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				learning >= 10
				trait = scholar
			}

			at_location = ROOT
			block_general_event_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					learning >= 10
					trait = scholar
				}

				at_location = ROOT
				block_general_event_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = my_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3540 # Demand

		piety = -10

		event_target:my_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pressured_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3541
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3541
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3540 # Ask nicely

		prestige = -10

		event_target:my_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = asked_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3541
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3541
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3540 # Bribe

		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = event_target:my_courtier
				value = 0.10
			}
		}

		event_target:my_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = bribed_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3541
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3541
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3540 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
	}
}

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

		trait = scholar

		NOR = {
			trait = cynical
			has_character_modifier = the_idle
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = yes

		any_courtier = {
			is_priest = yes

			OR = {
				trait = scholar
				learning >= 9
			}

			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 0
			}

			in_command_trigger = no
			at_location = ROOT
			block_general_event_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3543

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_priest = yes

				OR = {
					trait = scholar
					learning >= 9
				}

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 0
				}

				in_command_trigger = no
				at_location = ROOT
				block_general_event_trigger = no
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3544
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3544
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3543

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = the_idle
			months = 3
		}
	}

character_event = {
	id = 3546
	desc = EVTDESC3546
	picture = GFX_evt_family

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = scholar
		in_command_trigger = no

		any_child = {
			is_alive = yes
			is_adult = no
			practical_age >= 6

			NOR = {
				trait = content
				trait = slothful
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_adult = no
				practical_age >= 6

				NOR = {
					trait = content
					trait = slothful
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = scholar_child
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3546

		event_target:scholar_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = history_lesson

			character_event = {
				id = 3547
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3547
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3546

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = event_target:scholar_child
			months = 6
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3546

		event_target:scholar_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = legendary_story

			character_event = {
				id = 3547
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3547
			}
		}
	}
}

# Scholar: ROOT
character_event = {
	id = 3548
	desc = EVTDESC3548
	picture = GFX_evt_family

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3548

		trigger = { has_character_flag = embarrassed_child }

		clr_character_flag = embarrassed_child

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_embarrassed
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3548

		trigger = { has_character_flag = delighted_child }

		clr_character_flag = delighted_child

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					learning >= 6
					NOT = { trait = ambitious }
				}

				random_list = {
					40 = {
						add_trait_fully_ambitious_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38178 } # Notify guardian
						}
					}

					10 = {
						add_trait_fully_slothful_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38151 } # Notify guardian
						}
					}

					40 = {
						add_trait_fully_diligent_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38156 } # Notify guardian
						}
					}

					10 = {
						add_trait_fully_content_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38179 } # Notify parent
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { learning < 6 }

				random_list = {
					10 = {
						add_trait_fully_ambitious_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38178 } # Notify guardian
						}
					}

					40 = {
						add_trait_fully_slothful_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38151 } # Notify guardian
						}
					}

					10 = {
						add_trait_fully_diligent_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38156 } # Notify guardian
						}
					}

					40 = {
						add_trait_fully_content_effect = yes

						ROOT = {
							character_event = { id = 38179 } # Notify parent
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Scholar: The Intervention ###
character_event = {
	id = 3550
	desc = EVTDESC3550
	picture = GFX_evt_quarrel

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = scholar
		in_command_trigger = no

		OR = {
			trait = zealous
			trait = diligent
			trait = ambitious
		}

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_married = no }

			any_courtier = {
				is_adult = yes

				OR = {
					trait = envious
					trait = paranoid
					trait = wroth
				}

				NOT = { trait = scholar }
				in_command_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning >= 10
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3550

		trigger = { is_married = yes }

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3551
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3551
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3550

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3550

		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				is_adult = yes

				OR = {
					trait = envious
					trait = paranoid
					trait = wroth
				}

				NOT = { trait = scholar }
				in_command_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 50
				}
			}
		}

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_adult = yes

				OR = {
					trait = envious
					trait = paranoid
					trait = wroth
				}

				NOT = { trait = scholar }
				in_command_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 50
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3552
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3552
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3550

		scaled_wealth = 0.5

		random = {
			chance = 25
			remove_trait = scholar
		}
	}
}

### Gardener: Flower Power ###
character_event = {
	id = 3555
	desc = EVTDESC3555
	picture = GFX_evt_garden

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	is_married = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gardener
		in_command_trigger = no

		OR = {
			trait = kind
			trait = charitable
			trait = gregarious
		}

		is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = flower_power }

		spouse = {
			is_abroad = no
			prisoner = no
		}

		any_courtier = {
			is_opposite_sex = ROOT
			NOT = { is_married = ROOT }

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_female = yes }
				is_pregnant = no
			}
			trigger_else = {
				ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
			}

			age >= 20
			practical_age < 40
			is_abroad = no
			is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 30
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 30
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3555

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3556
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA3556
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3555

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_opposite_sex = ROOT
				NOT = { is_married = ROOT }

				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_female = yes }
					is_pregnant = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					ROOT = { is_pregnant = no }
				}

				age >= 20
				practical_age < 40
				is_abroad = no
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 30
				}

				reverse_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 30
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3556
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB3556
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 10

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_idiot
				who = spouse
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3555

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = flower_power
			months = 1
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gardener
		stewardship < 15

		OR = {
			trait = diligent
			trait = ambitious

			NOR = {
				trait = slothful
				trait = content
			}
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				diplomacy >= 8
				learning >= 10
				trait = gardener
			}

			is_adult = yes
			in_command_trigger = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning >= 9
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					learning >= 10
					diplomacy >= 8
					trait = gardener
				}

				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = target_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3560 # Demand

		piety = -10

		event_target:target_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pressured_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3561
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3561
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3560 # Ask nicely

		event_target:target_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = asked_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3561
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3561
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3560 # Bribe

		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = event_target:target_courtier
				value = 0.10
			}
		}

		event_target:target_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = bribed_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3561
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3561
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3560 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
	}
}

# Gardener: Courtier reacts to demands/bribes or being asked nicely
character_event = {
	id = 3561
	desc = EVTDESC3561
	picture = GFX_evt_garden

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3561

		trigger = { has_character_flag = pressured_scholar }

		clr_character_flag = pressured_scholar

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_disgruntled
				who = FROM
				years = 2
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = irritated_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3562
				days = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3562
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3561

		trigger = { has_character_flag = asked_scholar }

		clr_character_flag = asked_scholar

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = FROM
				years = 2
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = happy_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3562
				days = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3562
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3561

		trigger = { has_character_flag = bribed_scholar }

		clr_character_flag = bribed_scholar

		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
			from = FROM
			value = 0.10
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = generous_scholar

			character_event = {
				id = 3562
				days = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3562
			}
		}
	}
}

		clr_character_flag = happy_scholar
		change_stewardship = 2

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_delighted
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3562

		trigger = { has_character_flag = generous_scholar }

		clr_character_flag = generous_scholar
		change_stewardship = 1
	}
}

### Gardener: Spend too much money? ###
character_event = {
	id = 3563
	desc = EVTDESC3563
	picture = GFX_evt_garden

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gardener
		NOT = { trait = greedy }
		in_command_trigger = no

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_married = no }

			any_courtier = {
				trait = greedy
				stewardship >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			stewardship >= 10
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3563

		trigger = { is_married = yes }

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3564
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3564
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3563

		prestige = 10

		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait_depressed_effect = yes }
			10 = { remove_trait_gardener_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3563

		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				trait = greedy
				stewardship >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}
		}

		scaled_wealth = -0.15

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				trait = greedy
				stewardship >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3565
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3565
			}
		}
	}
}

### Gardener: The Bees! ###
character_event = {
	id = 3568
	desc = EVTDESC3568
	picture = GFX_evt_garden

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gardener
		health < 6
		is_ill = no
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_voter = {
			block_general_event_trigger = no

			OR = {
				trait = brave
				trait = diligent
				trait = ambitious
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3568

		random_voter = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				block_general_event_trigger = no

				OR = {
					trait = brave
					trait = diligent
					trait = ambitious
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3569
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3569
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3568

		trigger = {
			any_child = {
				practical_age >= 14

				OR = {
					trait = brave
					trait = diligent
					trait = ambitious
				}

				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
			}
		}

		random_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				practical_age >= 14

				OR = {
					trait = brave
					trait = diligent
					trait = ambitious
				}

				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3569
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3569
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3568

		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				OR = {
					trait = brave
					trait = diligent
					trait = ambitious
				}

				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
				is_councillor = no
			}
		}

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3569
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3569
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3568

		random_list = {
			40 = { }
			30 = { add_trait_wounded_effect = yes }
			30 = { give_ill_effect = yes }
			20 = { change_stewardship = 1 }
		}
	}
}

# Gardener: Courtier/spouse/child is asked to help remove beehive
character_event = {
	id = 3569
	desc = EVTDESC3569
	picture = GFX_evt_garden

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3569

		random_list = {
			40 = {
				FROM = { set_character_flag = beehive_removed }
			}

			30 = {
				add_trait_wounded_effect = yes

				tooltip = {
					opinion = {
						name = opinion_irritated
						who = FROM
						years = 1
					}
				}

				FROM = { set_character_flag = beehive_wounded }
			}

			20 = {
				give_ill_effect = yes

				tooltip = {
					opinion = {
						name = opinion_irritated
						who = FROM
						years = 1
					}
				}

				FROM = { set_character_flag = beehive_ill }
			}

			10 = { change_stewardship = 1 }
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					name = opinion_grateful
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}

			character_event = { id = 3670 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3569

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_coward
				who = FROM
				years = 1
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = 3671 }
		}
	}
}

### Mystic: Gain intrigue ###
character_event = {
	id = 3570
	desc = EVTDESC3570
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = mystic
		intrigue < 15

		NAND = {
			trait = slothful
			trait = content
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = intriguing_book }
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				learning >= 10
				intrigue >= 8
				trait = mystic
			}

			is_adult = yes
			in_command_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning >= 9
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					learning >= 10
					intrigue >= 8
					trait = mystic
				}

				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = target_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3570 # Demand

		piety = -10

		random = {
			chance = 25

			event_target:target_courtier = {
				show_scope_change = no

				set_character_flag = pressured_scholar

				character_event = {
					id = 3571
					days = 2
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3571
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3570 # Ask nicely

		prestige = -10

		random = {
			chance = 25

			event_target:target_courtier = {
				show_scope_change = no

				set_character_flag = asked_scholar

				character_event = {
					id = 3571
					days = 2
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3571
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3570 # Bribe

		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
			to = event_target:target_courtier
			value = 0.10
		}

		random = {
			chance = 25

			event_target:target_courtier = {
				show_scope_change = no

				set_character_flag = bribed_scholar

				character_event = {
					id = 3571
					days = 2
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3571
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3570 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
	}
}

### Mystic: Start ###
character_event = {
	id = 3575
	desc = EVTDESC3575
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = mystic
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_priest = yes
			religion = ROOT
			piety >= 50
			is_adult = yes
			at_location = ROOT
			in_command_trigger = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3575

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				is_priest = yes
				religion = ROOT
				piety >= 50
				is_adult = yes
				at_location = ROOT
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3576
				days = 1
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3576
			}
		}
	}

### Mystic: Alchemy - Start ###
character_event = {
	id = 3585
	desc = EVTDESC3585
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = mystic

		OR = {
			learning >= 8
			is_smart_trigger = yes
		}

		OR = {
			trait = diligent
			trait = ambitious

			NOR = {
				trait = slothful
				trait = content
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_flag = alchemy_set }
		in_command_trigger = no
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			stewardship >= 8
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			martial >= 10
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3585

		set_character_flag = fiddle_alchemy

		character_event = {
			id = 3586
			tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA3586
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3585

		set_character_flag = research_alchemy

		character_event = {
			id = 3586
			tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB3586
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3585

		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			15 = { add_trait_stressed_effect = yes }
			15 = { remove_trait = mystic }
		}
	}
}

# Mystic: fiddle with alchemy
character_event = {
	id = 3586
	desc = EVTDESC3586
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3586

		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = fiddle_alchemy }

			random_list = {
				70 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3587
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3587
					}
				}

				30 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3588
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3588
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3587
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3587
					}
				}

				50 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3588
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3588
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_character_flag = fiddle_alchemy
		clr_character_flag = research_alchemy
	}
}

# Mystic: Alchemy - wounded
character_event = {
	id = 3587
	desc = EVTDESC3587
	picture = GFX_evt_library

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = alchemy_set
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3587

		trigger = { is_married = yes }

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_worried
			who = spouse
			years = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3587

		trigger = { is_married = no }
	}

	after = {
		add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = ugly }
			}

			if = {
				limit = { trait = attractive }
				remove_trait = attractive
			}

			add_trait = ugly
		}
	}
}

### Impaler: New torture equipment - Start ###
character_event = {
	id = 3600
	desc = EVTDESC3600
	picture = GFX_evt_torture

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = impaler

		OR = {
			trait = wroth
			trait = deceitful
			trait = cynical
		}

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_married = no }

			any_courtier = {
				trait = greedy
				stewardship >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		NOR = {
			trait = depressed
			has_character_modifier = brazen_bull

			any_owned_bloodline = {
				has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_brazen_bull # Handled by special decision
				bloodline_is_active_for = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			stewardship >= 8
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			learning < 6
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3600

		trigger = { is_married = yes }

		scaled_wealth = -0.25

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = brazen_bull
			years = 5
		}

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3601
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3601
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3600

		prestige = -10

		random = {
			chance = 10
			add_trait_depressed_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3600

		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				trait = greedy
				stewardship >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}
		}

		scaled_wealth = -0.25
		clr_character_flag = gold_ten

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = brazen_bull
			years = 5
		}

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				trait = greedy
				stewardship >= 8
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3601
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3601
			}
		}
	}
}

### Impaler: Gain intrigue ###
character_event = {
	id = 3605
	desc = EVTDESC3605
	picture = GFX_evt_torture

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = impaler
		num_of_prisoners >= 1
		intrigue < 15
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		NAND = {
			trait = slothful
			trait = content
		}

		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			in_command_trigger = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no

			OR = {
				intrigue >= 8
				learning >= 10
				trait = impaler
			}

			OR = {
				martial >= 10
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning >= 9
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no

				OR = {
					intrigue >= 8
					learning >= 10
					trait = impaler
				}

				OR = {
					martial >= 10
					trait = wroth
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = impaler_teacher
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3605 # Demand

		piety = -10

		event_target:impaler_teacher = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pressured_teacher

			character_event = {
				id = 3606
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3606
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3605 # Ask nicely

		prestige = -10

		event_target:impaler_teacher = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = asked_teacher

			character_event = {
				id = 3606
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3606
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3605 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3605 # Bribe

		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = event_target:impaler_teacher
				value = 0.10
			}
		}

		event_target:impaler_teacher = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = bribed_teacher

			character_event = {
				id = 3606
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3606
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = EVTOPTA3607

		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag

			irritated_teacher = {
				clr_character_flag = irritated_teacher

				reverse_opinion = {
					name = opinion_disgruntled
					who = FROM
					years = 2
				}

				change_intrigue = 1
			}

			happy_teacher = {
				clr_character_flag = happy_teacher

				reverse_opinion = {
					name = opinion_delighted
					who = FROM
					years = 2
				}

				change_intrigue = 2
			}

			generous_teacher = {
				clr_character_flag = generous_teacher
				change_intrigue = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

### Impaler: Start ###
character_event = {
	id = 3610
	desc = EVTDESC3610
	picture = GFX_evt_torture

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = impaler
		num_of_prisoners >= 2
		in_command_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			prisoner = yes
			has_character_modifier = the_dungeon
			is_adult = yes
			is_female = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = kind
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ambition = obj_buddhist_reject_cruelty
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				prisoner = yes
				has_character_modifier = the_dungeon
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = confession_target
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3610

		event_target:confession_target = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3611
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3611
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_ambition = obj_buddhist_reject_cruelty }
			cancel_ambition = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3610

		trigger = { has_character_modifier = brazen_bull }

		event_target:confession_target = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = tortured_by_brazenbull

			character_event = {
				id = 3611
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3611
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_ambition = obj_buddhist_reject_cruelty }
			cancel_ambition = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3610

		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_trait_fully_kind_effect = yes
		}

		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_trait_fully_charitable_effect = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_ambition = obj_buddhist_reject_cruelty }
			remove_trait = impaler
			remove_trait_silently_cruel_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 10
				remove_trait_impaler_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Impaler: ROOT
character_event = {
	id = 3617
	desc = EVTDESC3617
	picture = GFX_evt_torture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3617 # Interested

		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }

			if = {
				limit = { same_sex = FROM }

				add_character_modifier = {
					name = mother_daughter
					years = 5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = mother_son
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { same_sex = FROM }

				add_character_modifier = {
					name = father_son
					years = 5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = father_daughter
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_proud
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random = {
				chance = 10
				add_trait = impaler
			}
		}
	}
}

### Duelist: Gain martial ###
character_event = {
	id = 3620
	desc = EVTDESC3620
	picture = GFX_evt_melee

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = duelist

		NOR = {
			trait = slothful
			trait = content
			has_character_modifier = averted_duel
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no

			OR = {
				martial >= 10
				trait = duelist
			}

			age >= 20
			is_abroad = no
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = wroth
		}

		# CK2Plus
		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_focus = focus_war
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no

				OR = {
					martial >= 10
					trait = duelist
				}

				age >= 20
				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
				at_location = ROOT
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = duelist_partner
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3620 # Demand

		piety = -10

		event_target:duelist_partner = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pressured_duelist

			character_event = {
				id = 3621
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3621
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3620 # Ask nicely

		prestige = -10

		event_target:duelist_partner = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = asked_duelist

			character_event = {
				id = 3621
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3621
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3620 # Bribe

		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = event_target:duelist_partner
				value = 0.10
			}
		}

		event_target:duelist_partner = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = bribed_duelist

			character_event = {
				id = 3621
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3621
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3620 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes

		random = {
			chance = 20
			remove_trait_duelist_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Duelist: ROOT gets +martial
character_event = {
	id = 3622
	desc = EVTDESC3622
	picture = GFX_evt_melee

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3622

		trigger = { has_character_flag = irritated_duelist }

		clr_character_flag = irritated_duelist

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disgruntled
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
			character_event = { id = WoL.11200 }
		}
		else = {
			change_martial = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3622

		trigger = { has_character_flag = happy_duelist }

		clr_character_flag = happy_duelist

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_delighted
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
			character_event = { id = WoL.11200 }
		}
		else = {
			change_martial = 2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3622

		trigger = { has_character_flag = generous_duelist }

		clr_character_flag = generous_duelist

		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
			character_event = { id = WoL.11200 }
		}
		else = {
			change_martial = 1
		}
	}
}
