character_event = { # TODO: Should this event be updated to use the standard dueling effects?
	id = 3625
	desc = EVTDESC3625
	picture = GFX_evt_melee

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 65
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = duelist
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = averted_duel }

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no
			age >= 20
			practical_age < 65

			OR = {
				martial >= 9 # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?
				trait = duelist
			}

			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value < 10
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value < 10
			}

			prisoner = no
			is_councillor = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				age >= 20
				practical_age < 65

				OR = {
					martial >= 9 # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?
					trait = duelist
				}

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value < 10
				}

				reverse_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value < 10
				}

				prisoner = no
				is_councillor = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
				NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
			}

			save_event_target_as = duelist_opponent
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3625

		event_target:duelist_opponent = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3626
				days = 1
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3626
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3625

		prestige = -10

		random = {
			chance = 25
			remove_trait_duelist_effect = yes
		}

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_coward
			who = event_target:duelist_opponent
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3625

		trigger = {
			job_marshal = {
				martial >= 6 # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?
				age >= 20
				can_be_maimed_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = wounded }
				prisoner = no
				is_abroad = no
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 10
			remove_trait_duelist_effect = yes
		}

		job_marshal = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_glad
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}

			if = {
				limit = { martial < 12 } # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?

				random_list = {
					40 = { add_maimed_trait_effect = yes }
					40 = { add_trait_wounded_effect = yes }

					10 = {
						event_target:duelist_opponent = {
							add_trait_wounded_effect = yes
						}
					}

					10 = {
						event_target:duelist_opponent = {
							add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					10 = { add_maimed_trait_effect = yes }
					20 = { add_trait_wounded_effect = yes }

					40 = {
						event_target:duelist_opponent = {
							add_trait_wounded_effect = yes
						}
					}

					30 = {
						event_target:duelist_opponent = {
							add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3630
	desc = EVTDESC3630
	picture = GFX_evt_melee

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = duelist

		NOR = {
			trait = craven
			has_character_modifier = averted_duel
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_married = no }

			any_courtier = {
				is_adult = yes

				OR = {
					martial >= 6
					trait = craven
				}

				NOT = { trait = duelist}
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wounded
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_female = yes
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3630

		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }

			spouse = {
				show_scope_change = no

				character_event = {
					id = 3631
					days = 2
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3631
					portrait = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_courtier = {
				show_scope_change = no

				limit = {
					OR = {
						martial >= 6
						trait = craven
					}

					is_adult = yes
					NOT = { trait = duelist }
					in_command_trigger = no
					is_inaccessible_trigger = no
				}

				character_event = {
					id = 3632
					days = 2
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3632
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3630

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			if = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = no
					is_abroad = no
				}

				opinion = {
					name = opinion_glad
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 20
			remove_trait_duelist_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3635
	desc = EVTDESC3635
	picture = GFX_evt_melee

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 20
	max_age = 65
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = duelist

		OR = {
			real_tier = DUKE
			real_tier = COUNT
		}

		NOR = {
			has_character_modifier = averted_duel
			has_character_modifier = master_duelist
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		top_liege = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				OR = {
					real_tier = DUKE
					real_tier = COUNT
				}

				OR = {
					trait = duelist
					martial >= 9 # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?
				}

				is_female = no
				age >= 20
				practical_age < 65
				can_be_maimed_trigger = yes
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value < -10
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = wounded
					trait = infirm
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		top_liege = {
			random_realm_province = {
				limit = {
					held_under_PREV = yes

					any_province_lord = {
						OR = {
							real_tier = DUKE
							real_tier = COUNT
						}

						OR = {
							trait = duelist
							martial >= 9 # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?
						}

						is_female = no
						age >= 20
						practical_age < 65
						can_be_maimed_trigger = yes
						is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							value < -10
						}

						NOR = {
							trait = wounded
							trait = infirm
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}

				save_event_target_as = duel_location
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3635

		event_target:duel_location = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random_province_lord = {
				show_scope_change = no

				limit = {
					OR = {
						real_tier = DUKE
						real_tier = COUNT
					}

					OR = {
						trait = duelist
						martial >= 9 # TODO: Shouldn't this be using combat_rating?
					}

					is_female = no
					age >= 20
					practical_age < 65
					can_be_maimed_trigger = yes
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no

					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value < -10
					}

					NOR = {
						trait = wounded
						trait = infirm
						character = ROOT
					}
				}

				character_event = {
					id = 3636
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3636
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3635

		add_trait_fully_silently_craven_effect = yes

		random = {
			chance = 20
			remove_trait_duelist_effect = yes
		}
	}

### Hunter: Gain martial ###
character_event = {
	id = 3640
	desc = EVTDESC3640
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = hunter
		martial < 15
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		NOR = {
			trait = slothful
			trait = craven
		}

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				martial >= 10
				trait = hunter
			}

			is_adult = yes
			at_location = ROOT
			in_command_trigger = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					martial >= 10
					trait = hunter
				}

				is_adult = yes
				at_location = ROOT
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = fellow_hunter
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3640 # Demand

		piety = -10

		event_target:fellow_hunter = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pressured_hunter

			character_event = {
				id = 3641
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3641
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3640 # Ask nicely

		prestige = -10

		event_target:fellow_hunter = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = asked_hunter

			character_event = {
				id = 3641
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3641
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3640 # Bribe

		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = event_target:fellow_hunter
				value = 0.10
			}
		}

		event_target:fellow_hunter = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = bribed_hunter

			character_event = {
				id = 3641
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3641
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3640 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes

		random = {
			chance = 20
			remove_trait_hunter_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

				who = FROM
				years = 2
			}
		}

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disgruntled

character_event = {
	id = 3650
	desc = EVTDESC3650
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = hunter

		NOR = {
			religion_group = muslim
			religion_group = jewish_group
			trait = craven
			has_character_modifier = master_hunter
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_voter = {
			OR = {
				has_job_title = job_marshal
				has_job_title = job_spymaster
			}

			OR = {
				trait = ambitious
				trait = diligent
			}

			is_adult = yes
			in_command_trigger = no
			at_location = ROOT
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3650

		trigger = {
			job_marshal = {
				OR = {
					trait = ambitious
					trait = diligent
				}

		}

		job_marshal = {

			}
		}
	}

	desc = EVTDESC3660
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events
#	show_root = yes

	ai = no
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = poet

		OR = {
			trait = charitable
			trait = gregarious

			NAND = {
				diplomacy >= 15
				trait = content
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_flag = poet_3660_triggered }
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = poet_3660_triggered

		create_character = {
			dynasty = random
			age = 30
			female = no
			random_traits = yes
			culture = ROOT
			religion = ROOT

			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 10
			}

			add_trait = poet
		}

		new_character = {
			give_nickname = nick_the_troubadour
			save_event_target_as = target_poet
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3660 # Demand

		piety = -10

		event_target:target_poet = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = pressured_poet

			character_event = {
				id = 3661
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3661
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3660 # Ask nicely

		prestige = -10

		event_target:target_poet = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = asked_poet

			character_event = {
				id = 3661
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3661
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3660 # Bribe

		tooltip = {
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = event_target:target_poet
				value = 0.10
			}
		}

		event_target:target_poet = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = bribed_poet

			character_event = {
				id = 3661
				days = 2
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3661
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3660 # Ignore

		add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
	}
}

# Poet: Courtier reacts to demands/bribes or being asked nicely
character_event = {
	id = 3661
	desc = EVTDESC3661
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3661

		trigger = { has_character_flag = pressured_poet }

		clr_character_flag = pressured_poet

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = irritated_poet

			character_event = {
				id = 3662
				days = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3662
			}
		}

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_disgruntled
				who = FROM
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3661

		trigger = { has_character_flag = asked_poet }

		clr_character_flag = asked_poet

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = happy_poet

			character_event = {
				id = 3662
				days = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3662
			}
		}

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = FROM
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3661

		trigger = { has_character_flag = bribed_poet }

		clr_character_flag = bribed_poet

		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
			from = FROM
			value = 0.10
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = generous_poet

			character_event = {
				id = 3662
				days = 7
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3662
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poet: ROOT gets +diplomacy
character_event = {
	id = 3662
	desc = EVTDESC3662
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3662

		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag

			irritated_poet = {
				clr_character_flag = irritated_poet

				reverse_opinion = {
					name = opinion_disgruntled
					who = FROM
					years = 2
				}

				change_diplomacy = 1
			}

			happy_poet = {
				clr_character_flag = happy_poet

				reverse_opinion = {
					name = opinion_delighted
					who = FROM
					years = 2
				}

				change_diplomacy = 2
			}

			generous_poet = {
				clr_character_flag = generous_poet
				change_diplomacy = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3665
	desc = EVTDESC3665
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = poet
		diplomacy >= 6
		NOT = { trait = wroth }
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			OR = {
				trait = gluttonous
				trait = greedy
				trait = wroth
			}

			is_adult = yes
			in_command_trigger = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3665

		piety = -10
		add_trait_fully_silently_lustful_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3665

		random_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = gluttonous
					trait = greedy
					trait = wroth
				}

				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_upset
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}

		add_trait_fully_silently_cynical_effect = yes
		remove_trait_silently_kind_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3665

		piety = 10

		any_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				trait = zealous

				OR = {
					trait = chaste
					trait = humble
					piety >= 100
				}

				is_adult = yes
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_approves
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}

		add_trait_fully_silently_zealous_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3665

		add_trait_fully_silently_wroth_effect = yes
	}
}

### Poet: Courtier asks for a poem ###
character_event = {
	id = 3675
	desc = EVTDESC3675
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = poet
		has_lover = no
		in_command_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			age >= 20
			prisoner = no
			has_lover = no
			NOT = { trait = poet }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = poem_author

		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				age >= 20
				prisoner = no
				has_lover = no
				NOT = { trait = poet }
			}

			save_event_target_as = poem_customer
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3675

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = poetry_timer
			days = 430
			hidden = yes
		}

		add_trait_fully_silently_charitable_effect = yes

		event_target:poem_customer = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}

			add_character_modifier = {
				name = used_poetry_timer
				days = 430
				hidden = yes
			}

			random = {
				chance = 50

				character_event = {
					id = 3680 # Courtier might claim liege's poem is his/hers!
					days = 7
					random = 420
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_married = yes
				is_female = no

				event_target:poem_customer = {
					is_female = yes
					practical_age < 30

					NOR = {
						trait = homosexual
						trait = celibate
					}
				}
			}

			spouse = {
				character_event = { id = 3676 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3675

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = poetry_timer
			days = 430
			hidden = yes
		}

		wealth = 10

		event_target:poem_customer = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_mildly_disappointed
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}

			add_character_modifier = {
				name = used_poetry_timer
				days = 430
				hidden = yes
			}

			random = {
				chance = 50

				character_event = {
					id = 3680 # Courtier might claim liege's poem is his/hers!
					days = 7
					random = 420
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3675

		prestige = 10

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = event_target:poem_customer
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3676
	desc = EVTDESC3676
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3676

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_forgive
				who = FROM
				years = 1
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = 3677 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3676

		trigger = { is_lover = FROM }

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_sad
			who = FROM
			years = 1
		}

		random_list = {
			70 = {
				FROM = {
					show_scope_change = no

					character_event = {
						id = 3677
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3677
					}
				}
			}

			20 = { }

			10 = {
				FROM = { save_event_target_as = target_lover }

				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }

					character_event = {
						id = WoL.1102
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP64045
					}
				}
				else = {
					character_event = {
						id = 64045
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP64045
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Poet: Courtier might claim liege's poem is his/hers! ###
character_event = {
	id = 3680
	desc = EVTDESC3680
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal

	is_triggered_only = yes # CleanSlate: Now fired directly from event 3675, rather than on_bi_yearly_pulse

	# only_playable = yes
	only_men = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		has_character_modifier = used_poetry_timer
		trait = deceitful
		has_lover = no
		in_command_trigger = no
		NOT = { trait = celibate }

		event_target:poem_author = {
			has_character_modifier = poetry_timer
			prisoner = no
			war = no
			in_command_trigger = no
		}

		any_courtier = {
			is_female = yes
			age >= 20
			is_valid_romance_target = ROOT
			has_lover = no
			prisoner = no
			is_abroad = no
			NOT = { trait = celibate }

			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 20
			}

			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 20
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
				age >= 20
				is_valid_romance_target = ROOT
				has_lover = no
				prisoner = no
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = celibate }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 20
				}

				reverse_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 20
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = sweetheart
		}

		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = poetry_timer
				is_adult = yes
				war = no
				in_command_trigger = no
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
			}

			save_event_target_as = poem_author
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3680

		event_target:sweetheart = {
			show_scope_change = no

			add_lover = ROOT
		}

		random = {
			chance = 10

			event_target:poem_author = {
				show_scope_change = no

				character_event = {
					id = 3681
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3681
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3680

		prestige = -10
		remove_trait = deceitful

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_glad
			who = event_target:sweetheart
			years = 10
		}
	}
}

# Poet: Poetry thief is confronted
character_event = {
	id = 3681
	desc = EVTDESC3681
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3681 # Confront

		prestige = 5

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_irritated
			who = FROM
			years = 2
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3682
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3682
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3681 # Seduced my little girl!

		trigger = {
			is_parent_of = event_target:sweetheart

			event_target:sweetheart = {
				NOT = { is_married = FROM }
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			imprison = ROOT
			set_character_flag = seduced_daughter
			character_event = { id = 3683 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3681 # Seduced my wife!

		trigger = { is_married = event_target:sweetheart }

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			imprison = ROOT
			set_character_flag = seduced_wife
			character_event = { id = 3683 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3681 # Forgive

		prestige = -5

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_forgive
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

#### Falconer: Bring-your-kids-to-hunt-day ###
character_event = {
	id = 3690
	desc = EVTDESC3690
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	is_married = yes
	min_age = 20
	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = falconer
		num_of_children >= 3
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		spouse = {
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}

		any_child = {
			practical_age >= 13
			practical_age < 20
			is_abroad = no
			is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				practical_age >= 13
				practical_age < 20
				is_abroad = no
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = hunting_child
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3690

		event_target:hunting_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3691
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3691
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3690

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = spouse
			years = 5
		}

		event_target:hunting_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3692
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3691
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3690

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_angry
			who = spouse
			years = 5
		}

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = event_target:hunting_child
			years = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3690

		trigger = {
			spouse = { trait = falconer }

			event_target:hunting_child = {
				trait = brave
				martial >= 10
			}
		}

		character_event = {
			id = 3697
			tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3697
		}
	}
}

# Falconer: Child is welcome to hunt with parent
character_event = {
	id = 3691
	desc = EVTDESC3691
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3691

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_glad
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random_list = {
				20 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3693
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3693 # Good hunt!
					}
				}

				30 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3694
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3693 # You shame me!
					}
				}

				20 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3695
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3694 # I am impressed!
					}
				}

				30 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3696
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3695 # Plucking flowers? What for?
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3691

		change_martial = -1
		change_stewardship = 1

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					name = opinion_disappointed
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3698
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3698
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falconer: Child is NOT welcome to hunt with parent
character_event = {
	id = 3692
	desc = EVTDESC3692
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3692

		opinion = {
			name = opinion_disappointed
			who = FROM
			years = 5
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random_list = {
				20 = {
					trigger = {
						event_target:hunting_child = {
							martial < 10
						}
					}

					character_event = {
						id = 3693
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3693 # Good hunt!
					}
				}

				30 = {
					character_event = {
						id = 3694
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3694 # You shame me!
					}
				}

				20 = {
					trigger = {
						event_target:hunting_child = {
							NOT = { trait = brave }
						}
					}

					character_event = {
						id = 3695
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3694 # I am impressed!
					}
				}

				30 = {
					trigger = {
						event_target:hunting_child = {
							learning < 10
						}
					}

					character_event = {
						id = 3696
						tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3695 # Plucking flowers? What for?
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3692

		change_martial = -1
		change_stewardship = 2

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					name = opinion_disappointed
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3698
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3698
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falconer: Good Hunt!
character_event = {
	id = 3693
	desc = EVTDESC3693
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3693

		change_martial = 1

		event_target:hunting_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion = {
					name = opinion_disappointed
					who = ROOT
				}
			}

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_glad
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}

			change_martial = 1
		}
	}
}

			}

			change_martial = 1

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_happy
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

### Falconer: Courtier asks for help with bird ###
character_event = {
	id = 3700
	desc = EVTDESC3700
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 20
	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = falconer
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			martial >= 6
			block_general_event_trigger = no

			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 20
			}

			NOR = {
				trait = falconer
				trait = craven
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				martial >= 6
				block_general_event_trigger = no

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 20
				}

				NOR = {
					trait = falconer
					trait = craven
				}
			}

			save_event_target_as = falcon_help
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3700

		add_trait_fully_silently_deceitful_effect = yes

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = sold_falcon

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_happy
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}

		random_list = {
			40 = {
				character_event = {
					id = 3701
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3701
				}
			}

			30 = {
				character_event = {
					id = 3702
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3702
				}
			}

			20 = { }
			10 = { change_intrigue = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3700

		wealth = 10

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_glad
			who = event_target:falcon_help
			years = 5
		}

		random_list = {
			30 = { }
			20 = { prestige = 10 }
			10 = { add_trait_wounded_effect = yes }
			20 = { add_trait_fully_charitable_effect = yes }
			20 = { add_trait_fully_greedy_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3700

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			set_character_flag = trained_falcon

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_delighted
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}

		random_list = {
			40 = {
				set_character_flag = good_bird

				character_event = {
					id = 3701
					days = 14
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3701
				}
			}

			30 = {
				set_character_flag = bad_bird

				character_event = {
					id = 3702
					days = 14
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3702
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3700

		prestige = -5

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			add_friend = ROOT
			set_character_flag = deceitful_falconer
		}

		character_event = {
			id = 3703
			days = 10
			random = 20
		}
	}
}

# Falconer: Good bird!
character_event = {
	id = 3701
	desc = EVTDESC3701
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3701 # Keep it

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = good_bird }
		}

		prestige = 10

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			clr_character_flag = sold_falcon

			random = {
				chance = 20

				set_character_flag = falcon_kept

				character_event = {
					id = 3704
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3704
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3701 # Train it and sell it

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = good_bird }
		}

		wealth = 20

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			clr_character_flag = sold_falcon

			random = {
				chance = 45

				set_character_flag = sold_falcon

				character_event = {
					id = 3704
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3704
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3701 # Good bird!

		trigger = { has_character_flag = good_bird }

		prestige = 20
		clr_character_flag = good_bird

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			clr_character_flag = trained_falcon

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3707
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3707
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falconer: Bad bird!
character_event = {
	id = 3702
	desc = EVTDESC3702
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3702

		trigger = { has_character_flag = bad_bird }

		add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			clr_character_flag = trained_falcon
			set_character_flag = untrainable_bird

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_sad
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3705
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA3705
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3702

		trigger = { has_character_flag = bad_bird }

		add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes

		random_list = {
			50 = { add_trait_fully_cruel_effect = yes }
			50 = { add_trait_fully_wroth_effect = yes }
		}

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			clr_character_flag = trained_falcon
			set_character_flag = killed_bird

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3705
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA3705
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3702 # Sell it back

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = bad_bird }
		}

		add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes
		wealth = 10

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			opinion = {
				name = opinion_disappointed
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3705
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB3705
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD3702 # Kill bird

		trigger = {
			any_courtier = {
				has_character_flag = sold_falcon
			}
		}

		add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes

		random_list = {
			50 = { add_trait_fully_cruel_effect = yes }
			50 = { add_trait_fully_wroth_effect = yes }
		}

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			clr_character_flag = sold_falcon

			random = {
				chance = 20

				set_character_flag = killed_falcon

				character_event = {
					id = 3705
					tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPB3705
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falconer:
character_event = {
	id = 3703
	desc = EVTDESC3703
	picture = GFX_evt_falconing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3703

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			imprison = ROOT
			character_event = { id = 3706 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3703

		prestige = -10

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}

			add_trait_fully_silently_content_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_trait_fully_silently_slothful_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3703

		event_target:falcon_help = {
			show_scope_change = no

			reverse_opinion = {
				name = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3706
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3706
			}
		}
	}
}

### GREGARIOUS ###

### Vassal does NOT support liege ###
character_event = {
	id = 3710
	desc = EVTDESC3710
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gregarious

		NAND = {
			trait = slothful
			trait = content
		}

		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_vassal = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value < -10
			}

			prisoner = no
			war = no
			in_command_trigger = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value < -10
				}

				prisoner = no
				war = no
				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = nonsupportive_vassal
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3710

		event_target:nonsupportive_vassal = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3711
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3711
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3710

		prestige = 10

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_upset
			who = event_target:nonsupportive_vassal
			years = 5
		}
	}
}

# Liege talks to vassal, vassal reacts
character_event = {
	id = 3711
	desc = EVTDESC3711
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3711

		tooltip = {
			opinion = {
				name = opinion_irritated
				who = FROM
				years = 1
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			show_scope_change = no

			tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					name = opinion_stubborn
					who = ROOT
					years = 1
				}
			}

			set_character_flag = vassal_stubborn

			character_event = {
				id = 3712
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPA3712
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3711

### Gregarious character's child is shy! ###
character_event = {
	id = 3715
	desc = EVTDESC3715
	picture = GFX_evt_guardian

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gregarious
		in_command_trigger = no

		any_child = {
			trait = shy
			is_adult = no
			is_abroad = no
			prisoner = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
				is_adult = no
				is_abroad = no
				prisoner = no
			}

			save_event_target_as = shy_child
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3715

		event_target:shy_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random_list = {
				25 = { remove_trait_shy_effect = yes }
				25 = { add_trait_fully_gregarious_effect = yes }
				30 = { add_trait_fully_paranoid_effect = yes }
				20 = { add_trait_stressed_effect = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3715

		event_target:shy_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random_list = {
				30 = { }
				25 = { add_trait_fully_paranoid_effect = yes }
				25 = { add_trait_fully_cynical_effect = yes }
				20 = { change_intrigue = 1 }
			}
		}

		add_trait_fully_cynical_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3715

		event_target:shy_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			random_list = {
				20 = { }

				10 = {
					opinion = {
						name = opinion_unhappy
						who = ROOT
						years = 5
					}
				}

				20 = { add_trait_depressed_effect = yes }
				25 = { change_learning = 1 }
				25 = { remove_trait_shy_effect = yes }
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 25
			add_trait_fully_content_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

### Take care of a courtier? ###
character_event = {
	id = 3720
	desc = EVTDESC3720
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_bi_yearly_pulse, random_events

	only_rulers = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = gregarious
		in_command_trigger = no
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no

		any_courtier = {
			trait = proud
			is_adult = yes

			OR = {
				trait = shy
				trait = paranoid
				trait = cynical
			}

			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				value >= 10
			}

			in_command = no
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				trait = proud
				is_adult = yes

				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = paranoid
					trait = cynical
				}

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 10
				}

				in_command_trigger = no
				is_inaccessible_trigger = no

			}

			save_event_target_as = proud_courtier
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3720

		event_target:proud_courtier = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3721
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3721
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3720

		random = {
			chance = 25

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { trait = slothful }
				}

				add_trait_fully_slothful_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { trait = content }
				}

				add_trait_fully_content_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				remove_trait_gregarious_effect = yes
			}
		}

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_upset
			who = event_target:proud_courtier
			years = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC3720

		reverse_opinion = {
			name = opinion_grateful
			who = event_target:proud_courtier
			years = 5
		}

		random = {
			chance = 25
			remove_trait_slothful_effect = yes
		}

		random = {
			chance = 25
			remove_trait_content_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 3750
	desc = EVTDESC3750
	picture = GFX_evt_jerusalem

	is_triggered_only = yes # on_five_year_pulse, random_events

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = muslim
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

	trigger = {
		trait = zealous
		in_command_trigger = no

		OR = {
			spouse = {
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}

			any_child = {
				practical_age >= 15
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			trait = gluttonous
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 3.0
			trait = envious
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			trait = kind
		}

		mult_modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA3750

		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				is_abroad = no
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}
		}

		spouse = {
			show_scope_change = no

			character_event = {
				id = 3751
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3751
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB3750

		trigger = {
			any_child = {
				practical_age >= 15
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}
		}

		random_child = {
			show_scope_change = no

			limit = {
				practical_age >= 15
				NOT = { trait = zealous }

				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value >= 100
				}
			}

			character_event = {
				id = 3751
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP3751
			}
		}
	}
}
